@@ignore\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 任务与调度体系 (TaskSystem & WorkerPool)\n// ============================================\n\n// Task（平台级任务）\n// 定义：跨 Worker、跨重试、带业务语义的任务\n// 职责：包含任务类型、业务对象关联、重试策略、优先级等平台级元信息\n// 关系：Task → Job（一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job，用于重试）\nmodel Task {\n  id             String     @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  type           TaskType\n  status         TaskStatus @default(PENDING)\n  payload        Json?\n  output         Json? // 任务输出结果，Engine/Worker 执行完成后写入\n  attempts       Int        @default(0)\n  maxRetry       Int        @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int        @default(0)\n  error          String?\n  workerId       String? // 实际执行该 Task 的 Worker 节点 ID\n  traceId        String? // Stage13-Final: Pipeline 级 @relation(\"ProjectTasks\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationTasks\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"TaskWorker\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([status, createdAt])\n}\n\n// WorkerJob（Worker 执行记录）\n// 定义：Worker 维度的一次具体执行记录\n// 职责：记录 Worker 执行任务的过程和结果\n// 关系：WorkerJob 与 Task/Job 是不同层面的概念，WorkerJob 主要用于 Worker 内部调度和计费\nmodel WorkerJob {\n  id            String          @id @default(uuid())\n  type          WorkerJobType\n  payload       Json // { Job（Worker 执行单元）\n// 定义：某个 Worker 在某个时间执行某个 Task 的一次尝试\n// 职责：记录单次执行的状态、结果、错误信息等\n// 关系：Job 属于某个 Task（taskId），一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job（用于重试）\n// Studio v0.2: Shot 生成任务模型\n// Studio v0.4: 增强队列化处理能力\n// Studio v0.8: 引入 Task 层，Job 关联 Task\nmodel ShotJob {\n  id             String    @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  episodeId      String\n  sceneId [organizationId], references: [id])\n}\n\nmodel WorkerNode {\n  id            String       @id @default(uuid())\n  workerId      String       @unique\n  name          String? // Worker 名称（可选）\n // Relations\n  project      Project            @relation(\"ProjectNovelSources\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  analysisJobs NovelAnalysisJob[]        String   @id @default(uuid())\n  novelSourceId  String\n  orderIndex     Int // 章节顺序（从1开始）\n  title          String // 章节标题\n  rawText        String   @db.Text // 章节原始文本（UTF-8）\n  summary        String?  @db.Text // S1-FIX-A: 引擎对章节的摘要，后续由小说分析引擎生成\n  startParagraph Int? // 起始段落索引（在原始文本中的位置）\n  endParagraph   Int? // 结束段落索引\n  characterCount Int? // 章节字符数\n  createdAt      DateTime @@map(\"scene_draft_status\")\n}\n\nmodel NovelAnalysisJob {\n  id            String               @id @default(uuid())\n  projectId     String\n  novelSourceId String?\n  chapterId     String? //     @relation(\"ProjectNovelAnalysisJobs\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  novelSource NovelSource? @relation(\"NovelSourceAnalysisJobs\", fields: [novelSourceId], @@ignore\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 任务与调度体系 (TaskSystem & WorkerPool)\n// ============================================\n\n// Task（平台级任务）\n// 定义：跨 Worker、跨重试、带业务语义的任务\n// 职责：包含任务类型、业务对象关联、重试策略、优先级等平台级元信息\n// 关系：Task → Job（一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job，用于重试）\nmodel Task {\n  id             String     @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  type           TaskType\n  status         TaskStatus @default(PENDING)\n  payload        Json?\n  output         Json? // 任务输出结果，Engine/Worker 执行完成后写入\n  attempts       Int        @default(0)\n  maxRetry       Int        @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int        @default(0)\n  error          String?\n  workerId       String? // 实际执行该 Task 的 Worker 节点 ID\n  traceId        String? // Stage13-Final: Pipeline 级 @relation(\"ProjectTasks\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationTasks\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"TaskWorker\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([status, createdAt])\n}\n\n// WorkerJob（Worker 执行记录）\n// 定义：Worker 维度的一次具体执行记录\n// 职责：记录 Worker 执行任务的过程和结果\n// 关系：WorkerJob 与 Task/Job 是不同层面的概念，WorkerJob 主要用于 Worker 内部调度和计费\nmodel WorkerJob {\n  id            String          @id @default(uuid())\n  type          WorkerJobType\n  payload       Json // { Job（Worker 执行单元）\n// 定义：某个 Worker 在某个时间执行某个 Task 的一次尝试\n// 职责：记录单次执行的状态、结果、错误信息等\n// 关系：Job 属于某个 Task（taskId），一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job（用于重试）\n// Studio v0.2: Shot 生成任务模型\n// Studio v0.4: 增强队列化处理能力\n// Studio v0.8: 引入 Task 层，Job 关联 Task\nmodel ShotJob {\n  id             String    @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  episodeId      String\n  sceneId [organizationId], references: [id])\n}\n\nmodel WorkerNode {\n  id            String       @id @default(uuid())\n  workerId      String       @unique\n  name          String? // Worker 名称（可选）\n @@map(\"novel_analysis_status\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// API Key 安全体系 (API Key Security System)\n// ============================================\n\n// API Key 模型（用于机器/Worker/外部服务认证）\n// 支持 HMAC + Nonce + Timestamp 签名机制\nmodel ApiKey {\n  id          String       @id @default(uuid())\n  key         String       @unique // 公钥 ID（对外暴露，例如：ak_xxx）\n  secretHash  String // 密钥哈希（使用 bcrypt 或类似算法，不存明文）\n  name        String? // 可选的 API Key 名称（便于管理）\n  ownerUserId String? // 可选，关联用户\n  ownerOrgId  String? // 可选，关联组织\n  status      ApiKeyStatus @default(ACTIVE) // 状态：ACTIVE / DISABLED\n  lastUsedAt  DateTime? // 最后使用时间\n  expiresAt   DateTime? // 过期时间（可选）\n  createdAt   DateTime     @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime     @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  ownerUser User?         @relation(\"UserApiKeys\", fields: [ownerUserId], references: [id])\n  ownerOrg  Organization? @relation(\"OrganizationApiKeys\", fields: [ownerOrgId], references: [id])\n  auditLogs AuditLog[]    @relation(\"ApiKeyAuditLogs\") // 审计日志关联\n\n  @@index([key])\n  @@index([status])\n  @@index([ownerUserId])\n  @@index([ownerOrgId])\n  @@map(\"api_keys\")\n}\n\nenum ApiKeyStatus {\n  ACTIVE\n  DISABLED\n\n  @@map(\"api_key_status\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 审计日志体系 (Audit Log System)\n// ============================================\n\n// 审计日志模型（用于记录关键操作）\n// 支持 JWT 用户和 API Key 两种认证来源\nmodel AuditLog {\n  id           String    @id @default(uuid())\n  userId       String? // JWT 用户 ID，可为空\n  apiKeyId     String? // 对应 ApiKey.id，可为空（HMAC 调用场景）\n  action       String // 动作标识：PROJECT_CREATED / TASK_CREATED / JOB_SUCCEEDED 等\n  resourceType String // 资源类型：project / episode / scene / shot / task / job / worker / auth 等\n  resourceId   String? // 资源主键 ID，可为空\n  ip           String? // 请求 IP\n  userAgent    String?   @db.Text // UA 字符串\n  // V1.1: 记录签名相关字段\n  nonce        String?\n  signature    String?\n  timestamp    DateTime?\n  details      Json? // 附加信息（请求参数、结果摘要等）\n  payload      Json? // S1-FIX-A: 规范向 payload：包含 action/resourceType/resourceId/ip/ua/nonce/signature/timestamp/details 等的完整快照\n  createdAt    DateTime  @default(now())\n\n  // Relations\n  user   User?   @relation(\"UserAuditLogs\", fields: [userId], references: [id])\n  apiKey ApiKey? @relation(\"ApiKeyAuditLogs\", fields: [apiKeyId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([createdAt])\n  @@index([action])\n  @@index([resourceType, resourceId])\n  @@index([userId])\n  @@index([apiKeyId])\n  @@index([nonce, timestamp])\n  @@map(\"audit_logs\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// Media & Security (ADD_SAFE
